## Session 17 — 2026-03-22 (/build mode continuation)

### Deliverable 1: Telegram Link Intake Pipeline (BehiqueBot)
- **File:** `modules/link_handler.py`
- **What:** Full pipeline — detect URLs in Telegram messages, scrape content (trafilatura -> BeautifulSoup -> Apify -> fallback), LLM triage into IDEA/PROJECT/REFERENCE/CONTENT/JOURNAL, write to vault files, register node in vault_graph.json, send formatted confirmation
- **Vault mapping:** IDEA -> IDEAS_BACKLOG.md | PROJECT -> PENDING_PROJECTS.md | REFERENCE -> 05-Knowledge/REFERENCES.md | CONTENT -> content-empire/CONTENT_CAPTURES.md | JOURNAL -> AI_JOURNAL.md
- **Secrets:** All keys via env vars (APIFY_API_KEY, OPENAI_API_KEY, OLLAMA_HOST) — nothing hardcoded
- **Integration:** Wired into main.py handle_text — pure URLs routed to link handler, mixed messages (URL + text) route both
- **Dependencies added:** `beautifulsoup4`, `trafilatura` in requirements.txt
- **Status:** DEPLOYED — syntax tested, all functions verified

### Deliverable 2: PDF conversions (9 products + 4 free lead magnets)
All PDFs complete: ai-employee-guide.pdf, roblox-builders-guide.pdf, 3d-fashion-guide.pdf, self-hosted-store-guide.pdf, social-media-pipeline-guide.pdf, ai-news-tracker-guide.pdf, solopreneur-os.pdf, behike-method-v2.pdf, ai-security-guide.pdf, prompt-engineering-cheat-sheet.pdf, free/5-ai-tools-lead-magnet.pdf, free/ai-safety-checklist.pdf, free/business-automation-audit.pdf, free/zero-dollar-ai-stack.pdf

## Wave 25 -- Audio-Reactive Brand + 3 New App Products [2026-03-22]

### Deliverable 104: tools/particle-brand/particle-audio-reactive.html -- REMIX 10
Audio-reactive particle brand component. Internal Web Audio synthesis (no mic). Three modes:
- Ambient (110/165/220Hz open fifth, slow LFO 0.4Hz, blue accent)
- Pulse (82/123/164Hz power chord, fast LFO 1.2Hz, green accent)
- Wave (196/261/329Hz major third, very slow LFO 0.18Hz, purple accent)
Face particles change color to match mode. Volume slider. Idle breathing animation before audio starts.
All analyser data fed from internal synthesis -- face reacts to generated sound, not mic.
